# 500000-500999 - Poland (Commonwealth)
# 	500000-500099 - Pre-Uprising + Uprising
# 	500100-500199 - Red-White
# 	500200-500599 - Commonwealth
# 	500600-500799 - Foreign Interventions (Austria, Prussia, France)
# 	500800-500899 - Vasa/Jagiellonian
# 	500900-500999 - Other Polish Stuff
# 501000-501999 - Russia (Panslavic)
# 502000-502999 - Russia (Zheltorossiya)
# 503000-503999 - Russia (Soviet)
# 504000-504999 - Russia (Great Game)
# 505000-505999 - Russia (Russian America)

## Setup + Uprising - ids 500000 - 500099
# Organic Statue of Poland
country_event = { 
	id = 500000
	title = "EVTNAME500000"
	desc = "EVTDESC500000"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CPL
		year = 1836
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA500000"
		add_country_modifier = { name = rus_organic_statute_cpl duration = -1 }
		set_country_flag = poland_content
	}
}

# Russia Trigger Event
country_event = {
	id = 500001
	title = "EVTNAME500001"
	desc = "EVTDESC500001"
	news = yes
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC95076_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC95076_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC95076_NEWS_SHORT"
	picture = "january_uprising"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA500001"
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_happened
		set_country_flag = through_january_uprising
		
		CPL = {
			treasury = 50000
			leadership = 80
			add_country_modifier = { name = polish_uprising_mobilization duration = 2920 }

			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = military_school_of_poland
					}
				}
				owner = {
					define_general = {
						name = "Stanislaw Brzska"
						personality = spirited
						background = compassionate_priest
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Aleksander Waszkowski"
						personality = steadfast
						background = nationalist
					}
				
					define_general = {
						name = "Francesco Nullo"
						personality = unflinching
						background = uncommonly_young
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Francois Rochebrune"
						personality = daring
						background = adventurer
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Marian Langiewicz"
						personality = implacable
						background = school_of_the_bayonet
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Romuald Traugutt"
						personality = defiant
						background = school_of_defense
					}
				}
			}

			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = military_school_of_poland }
					}
				}
				owner = {
					define_general = {
						name = "Stanislaw Brzska"
						personality = gutsy
						background = generals_aide
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Aleksander Waszkowski"
						personality = stouthearted
						background = war_college
					}
				
					define_general = {
						name = "Francesco Nullo"
						personality = unflinching
						background = uncommonly_young
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Francois Rochebrune"
						personality = disciplined
						background = innovative_tactician
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Marian Langiewicz"
						personality = harsh
						background = school_of_offense
					}

					define_general = {
						name = "Romuald Traugutt"
						personality = stout
						background = generals_aide
					}
				}
			}

			change_variable = {
				which = polish_whites_strength 
				value = 15
			}

			change_variable = {
				which = polish_reds_strength
				value = 10
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = hidden_tooltip
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = hidden_tooltip } }
			owner = {
				JAN = {
					country_event = 500612
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = hidden_tooltip

		release_vassal = LIT
		3399 = { secede_province = LIT }
		360 = { secede_province = RUS }
		936 = { secede_province = RUS }
		938 = { secede_province = RUS }
		361 = { secede_province = RUS }
		3510 = { secede_province = RUS }
		3511 = { secede_province = RUS }
		
		LIT = {
			treasury = 50000
			leadership = 80

			define_general = {
				name = "Antanas Mackevicius"
				personality = daring
				background = compassionate_priest
			}

			define_general = {
				name = "Zigmantas Sierakauskas"
				personality = daring
				background = expert_raider
			}
				
			define_general = {
				name = "Konstantinas Kalinauskas"
				personality = chivalrous
				background = young_genius
			}

			define_general = {
				name = "Boleslaw Kayeton Cologna"
				personality = cautious
				background = school_of_defense
			}

			add_country_modifier = { name = polish_uprising_mobilization duration = 2920 }
		}

		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core = POL
					is_core = LIT
					is_core = LAT
					is_core = BYE
					is_core = UKR
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = polish_revolt duration = 1080 } # This is so armies are slowed and Poland player has time to organize

			any_pop = { # This represents Polish Intelligentsia and Nobility in Lithuania and Belarus
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_pop_culture = lithuanian
						has_pop_culture = polish
					}
					OR = {
						strata = rich
						type = clergymen
					}
				}
				ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = liberal }
				militancy = 7
				consciousness = 8
			}
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500002 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# France Intervention
country_event = {
	id = 500002
	title = "EVTNAME500002"
	desc = "EVTDESC500002"
	picture = "january_uprising"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Intervene
		name = "EVTOPTA500002"
		set_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_intervening_power
		set_global_flag = CPL_january_intervention

		prestige = 15
		treasury = -100000

		create_alliance = CPL
		leave_alliance = RUS
		relation = { who = RUS value = -150 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = 200 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = 100 }

		CPL = {
			treasury = 90000
			small_arms = 250
			ammunition = 250
			canned_food = 250
			artillery = 100
			change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = 15 }
		}

		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = -10
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = austrian_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500003 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prussian_content
				AUS = { exists = no }
				KUK = { exists = no }
			}
			set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_AUS_done
			country_event = { id = 500005 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Material Support
		name = "EVTOPTB500002"
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_FRA_done
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_path_to_poland_done

		prestige = 5
		treasury = -25000
		
		relation = { who = RUS value = -100 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = 100 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = 50 }

		CPL = {
			treasury = 20000
			small_arms = 50
			ammunition = 50
			canned_food = 50
			artillery = 25
			change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = 5 }
		}
		
		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 4
			militancy = -6
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = austrian_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500004 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prussian_content
				AUS = { exists = no }
				KUK = { exists = no }
			}
			set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_AUS_done
			country_event = { id = 500005 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Neutrality
		name = "EVTOPTC500002"
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_FRA_done
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_path_to_poland_done

		prestige = -20

		relation = { who = RUS value = 50 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = -100 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = -100 }

		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = austrian_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500004 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prussian_content
				AUS = { exists = no }
				KUK = { exists = no }
			}
			set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_AUS_done
			country_event = { id = 500005 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# Austrian Intervention - French Intervention
country_event = {
	id = 500003
	title = "EVTNAME500003"
	desc = "EVTDESC500003"
	picture = "january_uprising"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Intervene
		name = "EVTOPTA500003"

		prestige = 15
		treasury = -100000

		create_alliance = FROM
		create_alliance = CPL
		leave_alliance = RUS
		relation = { who = RUS value = -150 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = 200 }
		relation = { who = FROM value = 200 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = 100 }

# Prussian Intervention
country_event = {
	id = 500005
	title = "EVTNAME500005"
	desc = "EVTDESC500005"
	picture = "january_uprising"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Alvensleben Convention
		name = "EVTOPTA500005"
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_PRU_done
		
		relation = { who = RUS value = 50 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = -150 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = -100 }

		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 10
			militancy = 10
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = russian_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500006 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention }
			}
			country_event = { id = 500009 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention
			}
			country_event = { id = 500016 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = british_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500017 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Neutrality
		name = "EVTOPTB500005"
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_alvensleben_done
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_PRU_done
		
		relation = { who = RUS value = 15 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = -50 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = -50 }

		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = 5
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention }
			}
			country_event = { id = 500009 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention
			}
			country_event = { id = 500016 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = british_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500017 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Support Poland
		name = "EVTOPTC500005"
		set_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
		set_country_flag = CPL_january_intervening_power
		set_global_flag = CPL_january_intervention
		set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_alvensleben_done

		create_alliance = CPL
		leave_alliance = RUS
		relation = { who = RUS value = -200 }
		relation = { who = CPL value = 200 }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = CPL value = 100 }

		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
			consciousness = 5
			militancy = -10
		}

		CPL = {
			change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = 15 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention }
			}
			country_event = { id = 500009 days = 3 }
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = french_content
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_french_intervention
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_german_intervention
			}
			country_event = { id = 500016 days = 3 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = british_content
			}
			country_event = { id = 500017 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# RUS - Alvensleben Convention
country_event = {
	id = 500006
	title = "EVTNAME500006"
	desc = "EVTDESC500006"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA500006"
		set_global_flag = alvensleben_convention

		relation = { who = FROM value = 50 }
		
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = 500007 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB500006"

		relation = { who = FROM value = -50 }
		
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = 500008 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# PRU - RUS Accepted Alvensleben
country_event = {
	id = 500007
	title = "EVTNAME500007"
	desc = "EVTDESC500007"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {

				any_greater_power = {
					rank = 5
					has_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
				}
				any_greater_power = {
					rank = 6
					has_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
				}
				any_greater_power = {
					rank = 7
					has_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
				}
				any_greater_power = {
					rank = 8
					has_country_flag = CPL_january_decision_made
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_repeating_intervention_done
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = russian_content
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_FRA_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_AUS_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_PRU_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_repeating_intervention_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_alvensleben_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_path_to_poland_done
				has_global_flag = CPL_january_intervention
			}
			country_event = { id = 500046 days = 10 }
		}

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = russian_content
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_FRA_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_AUS_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_ENG_PRU_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_repeating_intervention_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_alvensleben_done
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_chain_path_to_poland_done
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CPL_january_intervention }
			}
			country_event = { id = 500047 days = 10 }
		}
	}

#Event for Russia to decide what to do with szlachta after Poland is defeated
country_event = {
	id = 500048
	title = "EVTNAME500048"
	desc = "EVTDESC500048"
	picture = "vacation_on_siberia"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = january_uprising_happened
		has_country_flag = through_january_uprising
		CPL = { exists = no }
		LIT = { exists = no }
		owns = 706
		war = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

	option = { # punish them
		name = "EVTOPTA500048"
		set_global_flag = polish_uprising_crushed

		any_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
				NOT = { alliance_with = THIS }
			}
			relation = { who = THIS value = -25 }
		}

		add_tax_relative_income = 30

		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = POL }
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					OR = {
						pop_type = officers
						pop_type = capitalists
						pop_type = aristocrats
					}
				}
				reduce_pop = 0.7
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					pop_type = soldiers
				}
				reduce_pop = 0.8
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = russification duration = -1 } 
			add_province_modifier = { name = national_assimilation_complete duration = 7000 } # This is so U01 gets removed after 20 years
		}

		any_owned = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { is_core = CPL is_core = LIT }
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = polish }
				random_list = {
					25 = { reduce_pop = 0.99 }
					25 = { reduce_pop = 0.985 }
					25 = { reduce_pop = 0.98 }
					25 = { reduce_pop = 0.975 }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
	}

	option = { # be lenient
		name = "EVTOPTB500048"
		set_global_flag = polish_uprising_crushed
		set_country_flag = lenient_on_poles

		prestige = -60
		
		any_pop = {
			limit = { is_accepted_culture = no }
			consciousness = 6
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 500049
	title = "EVTNAME500049" # Polish petitions for annexation
	desc = "EVTDESC500049"
	picture = "greatpowers"

	trigger = {
		primary_culture = polish
		ai = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_integration_asked }
		is_greater_power = no
		war = no
		OR = {
			part_of_sphere = no
			in_sphere = POL
		}
		POL = {
			NOT = { truce_with = THIS }
			exists = yes
			neighbour = THIS
			is_vassal = no
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 28 }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA500049"
		set_country_flag = polish_integration_asked
		all_core = {
			add_core = POL
			remove_core = THIS
		}
		annex_to = POL

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = DZG
					is_secondary_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB500049"
		set_country_flag = polish_integration_asked
		all_core = { add_core = POL }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					tag = DZG
					is_secondary_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

# Negotiations - Religion
country_event = {
	id = 500053
	title = "EVTNAME500053"
	desc = "EVTDESC500053"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Agree to protect the Catholic Church in Poland
		name = "EVTOPTA500053"

		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				religion = orthodox
			}
			militancy = 1
		}

		add_country_modifier = { name = orthodox_church_protests duration = 1095 }
		
		change_variable = { which = towarzystwo_rolnicze_satisfied value = 5 }
		
		country_event = { id = 500054 days = 28 }
	}
	
	option = { # Russia is an Orthodox nation and shall continue to be an Orthodox nation
		name = "EVTOPTB500053"

	}

			}

		}

			owner = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = towarzystwo_rolnicze_satisfied value = 99.99 } }

		}

			}

		}

			owner = {

			}

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 500063
	title = "EVTNAME500063"
	desc = "EVTDESC500063"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Expand Secret Societies
		name = "EVTOPTA500063"
		
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 0 } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 0.25 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 0 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 3 } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 0.5 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 3 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 6 } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 0.75 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 6 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 8 } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 8 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 1.5 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = CPL_secret_societies value = 10 }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = { which = january_uprising_readiness value = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Spread Nationalist Propaganda
		name = "EVTOPTB500063"
		
	}
	
	option = { # Train/Recruit Underground Militias
		name = "EVTOPTC500063"
		
		change_variable = { which = CPL_military value = 1 }
	}
	
	option = { # Contact Foreign Exiles
		name = "EVTOPTD500063"
		
		change_variable = { which = CPL_foreign_powers value = 0.5 }
	}
	
	option = { # Next
		name = "EVTOPTE500063"
		
		
		country_event = 500064
	}
	
}

			exists = yes
			OR = {

				vassal_of = THIS
			}
		}
		any_owned_province = {
			is_core = CPL
		}
	}

		days = 3
	}

		name = "EVTOPTA500092"
		
		any_owned = {

				is_core = CPL
			}
			secede_province = CPL
		}
	}

# Serfdom Question - Poland
country_event = {
	id = 500103
	title = "EVTNAME500103"
	desc = "EVTDESC500103"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Compensation
		name = "EVTOPTA500103"
		political_reform = peonage
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = poor }
			militancy = 3
			consciousness = 3
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = rich }
			militancy = 1
			consciousness = 1
		}
		change_variable = { 
			which = polish_whites_strength
			value = 20
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = promised_compensation duration = -1 }

		set_country_flag = hidden_tooltip
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = hidden_tooltip } }
			owner = {
				JAN = {
					country_event = 500612
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = hidden_tooltip

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
	
	option = { # No Compensation
		name = "EVTOPTB500103"
		political_reform = peonage
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = poor }
			militancy = -3
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = rich }
			militancy = 5
			consciousness = 5
		}
		change_variable = { 
			which = polish_reds_strength
			value = 20
		}

		set_country_flag = hidden_tooltip
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = hidden_tooltip } }
			owner = {
				JAN = {
					country_event = 500612
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = hidden_tooltip

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Serfdom
		name = "EVTOPTC500103"
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = poor }
			militancy = 7
			consciousness = 7 
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { strata = rich }
			militancy = -1
			consciousness = -1
		}
		set_global_flag = polish_serfdom

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = habsburg_poland

# Nationalization 1
country_event = { 
	id = 500601
	title = "EVTNAME500601"
	desc = "EVTDESC500601"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Nationalize Foreign Factories
		name = "EVTOPTA500601" 
		add_country_modifier = { name = factory_debuff duration = 30 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = asked_for_aid_recently duration = 30 }

		change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = austrian_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = -5 }
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Remove Military Advisors
		name = "EVTOPTB500601"
		add_country_modifier = { name = military_debuff duration = 30 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = asked_for_aid_recently duration = 30 }

		change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = austrian_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = -5 }

				war = yes
			}
		}

# Nationalization 2
country_event = { 
	id = 500602
	title = "EVTNAME500602"
	desc = "EVTDESC500602"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Increase Tariffs
		name = "EVTOPTA500602"
		add_country_modifier = { name = tariffs_debuff duration = 30 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = asked_for_aid_recently duration = 30 }

		change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = austrian_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = -5 }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { money = 100000 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { money = 50000 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { money = 25000 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				NOT = { money = 10000 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB500602" # Expel Scientists
		add_country_modifier = { name = research_debuff duration = 30 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = asked_for_aid_recently duration = 30 }

		change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = austrian_influence_poland value = -5 }
		change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = -5 }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				literacy = 0.8
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { literacy = 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				NOT = { literacy = 0.25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				NOT = { literacy = 0.1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC500602" # Assert Ourselves
		badboy = 1
		any_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_greater_power = yes neighbour = THIS } }
			relation = { who = THIS value = -25 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = asked_for_aid_recently duration = 30 }

		change_variable = { which = french_influence_poland value = -10 }
		change_variable = { which = austrian_influence_poland value = -10 }
		change_variable = { which = prussian_influence_poland value = -10 }
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				badboy = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				badboy = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				badboy = 24
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD500602" # Close

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Triggered Updater for Red-White Struggle
country_event = {
	id = 500612
	title = "EVTNAME500612"
	desc = "EVTDESC500612"
	picture = "placeholder"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA500612"
		706 = {
			owner = {
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = poland_content
							check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 0 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 19.99 } }
							check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 0 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 19.99 } }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = poland_redwhite_aa duration = -1 }
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ab
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ac
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ad
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ba
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bb
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bd
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ca
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cb
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cd
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_da
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_db
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_dc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_dd
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = poland_content
							check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 0 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 19.99 } }
							check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 19.99 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 39.99 } }
						}
					}
					owner = {
						add_country_modifier = { name = poland_redwhite_ab duration = -1 }
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_aa
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ac
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ad
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ba
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bb
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_bd
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_ca
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cb
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_cd
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_da
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_db
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_dc
						remove_country_modifier = poland_redwhite_dd
					}
				}
				random_owned = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = poland_content
							check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 0 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_whites_strength value = 19.99 } }
							check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 39.99 } 
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = polish_reds_strength value = 69.99 } }
						}
					}

country_event = {
	id = 666666004
	title = "EVTNAME666666004"
	desc = "EVTDESC666666004a"
	picture = "greater_poland_uprising"
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = PZN
		OR = {
			# AND = {
			# 	year = 1846
			# 	month = 2
			# } # moved to a different event
			AND = {
				year = 1848
				month = 3
				has_global_flag = liberal_revolution_somewhere
				has_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising_suppressed
			}
			# KRA = {
			# 	has_global_flag = krakow_uprising

			# 		war_with = GCF

			# 		has_global_flag = january_uprising_decision
			# 		has_global_flag = january_uprising_happened
			# 	}
			# 	OR = {
			# 		war_with = RUS
			# 		has_global_flag = greater_poland_succeeded
			# 	}
			# }
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising }
	}
	
	# validator says shit shit doesn't work, but it actually does.
	immediate = { any_country = { limit = { OR = { tag = KRA tag = CPL } ai = no exists = yes } country_event = 666666123 } }
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB666666004"
		set_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising
		prestige = 25
		
		government = presidential_dictatorship
		ruling_party_ideology = liberal
		nationalvalue = nv_liberty
		political_reform = none_voting
		political_reform = harassment
		political_reform = appointed
		political_reform = state_controlled
		political_reform = free_press
		political_reform = yes_meeting
			
		primary_culture = polish
		remove_accepted_culture = north_german
				
		define_general = {
			name = "Ludwik Mieroslawski"
			personality = audacious
			background = nationalist
		}
		
		any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = polish_culture_group } militancy = -4 consciousness = -4 }
			
		add_country_modifier = { name = polish_uprising_mobilization duration = 2920 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = unrecognized_country duration = 1095 }
		
		AUS = {
			relation = { who = THIS value = -300 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -300 }
		}
		RUS = {
			relation = { who = THIS value = -300 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -300 }
			any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_culture = polish } militancy = 3 consciousness = 5 }
		}
		CPL = {
			any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_culture = polish } consciousness = 3 }
			relation = { who = THIS value = 100 }
			country_event = { id = 666666125 days = 10 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
			exists = yes
				OR = {
					tag = PRU
					tag = NGF
					tag = GER
					tag = GCF
				}
				owns = 549
			}
			release_vassal = THIS
			relation = { who = THIS value = -400 }
			diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -400 }
			any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_culture = polish } militancy = 2 consciousness = 4 }
			country_event = { id = 666666005 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				year = 1848
				has_global_flag = liberal_revolution_somewhere
				has_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising_suppressed
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA666666004" 
		set_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising_suppressed
		prestige = -25
		any_pop = { limit = { is_primary_culture = yes } militancy = 7 consciousness = 8 }
		# random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = yes } } owner = { THIS = { all_core = { add_core = PRU } } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

# Posen uprising response
country_event = {
	id = 666666012
	title = "EVTNAME666666012" # Polish defeated
	desc = "EVTDESC666666012"
	picture = "greater_poland_uprising"
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		PZN = { exists = no }
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			tag = PRU
			tag = NGF
			tag = GER
			tag = GCF
		}
		owns = 699
		owns = 701
		owns = 700
		has_global_flag = greater_poland_uprising
		has_country_flag = through_greater_poland_uprising
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPT666666012A"  # punish them
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes is_greater_power = yes capital_scope = { continent = europe } NOT = { alliance_with = THIS } }
			relation = { who = THIS value = -25 }
		}
		
		add_tax_relative_income = 15
		
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = PZN }
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					OR = {
						pop_type = officers
						pop_type = soldiers
						pop_type = aristocrats
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.85 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.80 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.75 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.7 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.65 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 85 }
	}
			
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPT666666012B"	# be lenient
		prestige = -30
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { is_accepted_culture = no }
			consciousness = 6
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
	}
			
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPT666666012C"
		badboy = 5
		any_country = {
			limit = { exists = yes is_greater_power = yes capital_scope = { continent = europe } NOT = { alliance_with = THIS } }
			relation = { who = THIS value = -50 }
		}
		
		add_tax_relative_income = 10
		
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = PZN }
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					OR = {
						pop_type = officers
						pop_type = soldiers
						pop_type = aristocrats
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.6 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.55 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.5 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.55 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.4 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = PZN }
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							pop_type = officers
							pop_type = soldiers
							pop_type = aristocrats
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.7 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.75 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.8 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.85 }
					20 = { reduce_pop = 0.9 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}
}

# PNC Formation
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # 
country_event = {
	id = 666666036
	title = "EVTNAME666666036"
	desc = "EVTDESC666666036"
	picture = "january_uprising"
	news = yes
	news_title = "EVTNAME666666036_NEWS_TITLE"
	news_desc_long = "EVTDESC666666036_NEWS_LONG"
	news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC666666036_NEWS_MEDIUM"
	news_desc_short = "EVTDESC666666036_NEWS_SHORT"
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CPL
			tag = KRA
			tag = PZN
		}
		exists = yes
		ai = no
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = krakow_uprising
			has_global_flag = krakow_war
			has_global_flag = krakow_succeeded
		}
		OR = {
			war_with = PRU
			war_with = NGF
			war_with = GER
			war_with = GCF
			war_with = AUS
			war_with = KUK
			war_with = SGF
			war_with = RUS
			AND = {
				war = no
				has_global_flag = january_uprising_succeeded
			}
			AND = {
				war = no
				has_global_flag = krakow_succeeded
			}
			AND = {
				war = no
				has_global_flag = greater_poland_succeeded
			}
		}
		POL = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = form_PNC }
		PZN = { exists = yes }
		GLM = { exists = yes }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 } 
	
	# events to inherit polish countries, validator says shit shit doesn't work, but it actually does.
	immediate = {
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = no OR = { tag = CPL tag = PZN } KRA = { exists = yes ai = yes } } } owner = { KRA = { country_event = 666666122 } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = no OR = { tag = CPL tag = KRA } PZN = { exists = yes ai = yes } } } owner = { PZN = { country_event = 666666122 } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = no OR = { tag = CPL tag = KRA } GLM = { exists = yes ai = yes } } } owner = { GLM = { country_event = 666666122 } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = no OR = { tag = KRA tag = PZN } CPL = { exists = yes ai = yes } } } owner = { CPL = { country_event = 666666122 } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ai = no OR = { tag = GLM tag = PZN } CPL = { exists = yes ai = yes } } } owner = { GLM = { country_event = 666666122 } } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPT666666036A"
		set_global_flag = form_PNC
		all_core = { add_core = POL }
		random_owned = { limit = { province_id = 706 } owner = { capital = 706 } } # Warsaw
		change_tag = POL
		
		government = presidential_dictatorship
		ruling_party_ideology = liberal
		nationalvalue = nv_liberty
		political_reform = none_voting
		political_reform = harassment
		political_reform = appointed
		political_reform = state_controlled
		political_reform = free_press
		political_reform = yes_meeting
			
		add_country_modifier = { name = polish_uprising_mobilization duration = 2920 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = unrecognized_country duration = 1095 }
		
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = PRU
					tag = NGF
					tag = GER
					tag = GCF
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			end_war = PZN
			end_war = THIS
			country_event = 666666009
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = KUK
					tag = SGF
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			end_war = KRA
			end_war = THIS
			country_event = 666666010
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = KUK
					tag = SGF
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			end_war = GLM
			end_war = THIS
			country_event = 666666010
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				exists = yes
			}
			end_war = CPL
			end_war = THIS
			country_event = 666666011
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						vassal_of = PRU
						substate_of = PRU
						vassal_of = NGF
						substate_of = NGF
						vassal_of = GER
						substate_of = GER
						vassal_of = GCF
						substate_of = GCF
						vassal_of = AUS
						substate_of = AUS
						vassal_of = KUK
						substate_of = KUK
						vassal_of = SGF
						substate_of = SGF
						vassal_of = RUS
						substate_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { overlord = { release = THIS } }
		}
		all_core = { add_core = POL }
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		any_country = { limit = { war_with = THIS } end_war = THIS }
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		any_country = { limit = { war_with = FROM } end_war = FROM }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVT666666122OPTA"
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		FROM = { inherit = THIS }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

# uprising
country_event = {
	id = 203903 # todolocalization
	title = "EVTNAME203903"
	desc = "EVTDESC203903"
	picture = "ferdinand"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = POL
			tag = PLC
		}
		has_country_modifier = russian_absolutist_encroachment
		is_vassal = no
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA203903"
		prestige = 5
		remove_country_modifier = russian_absolutist_encroachment
		remove_accepted_culture = russian
		remove_accepted_culture = ukrainian
		clr_country_flag = soc_reform_blocker
		clr_country_flag = pol_reform_blocker
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}
